This also motivates the child to want to get higher awards and better marks.\r\n\r\nThere are 39 subtopics categorized as follows:\r\n\r\nNumbers\r\n\r\n1.\tWrite\r\n2.\tCounting in Powers of 10\r\n3.\tPlace Value\r\n4.\tRounding\r\n5.\tCompare\r\n6.\tPrime\r\n7.\tSquare and Cube\r\n8.\tRoman Numerals\r\n\r\nCalculations\r\n\r\n9.\tAddition\r\n10.\tSubtraction\r\n11.\tMultiplication\r\n12.\tDivision\r\n13.\tEstimating\r\n14.\tSolve Problems\r\n\r\nFractions\r\n\r\n15.\t Simplify\r\n16.\tAddition\r\n17.\tSubtraction\r\n18.\tMultiplication\r\n19.\tConvert\r\n20.\tSolve Problems\r\n\r\nDecimals\r\n\r\n21.\t Addition\r\n22.\t Subtraction\r\n23.\tDividing by 10 or 100\r\n24.\t Place Value\r\n25.\t Rounding\r\n26.\t Compare\r\n27.\tConvert\r\n28.\t Solve Problems\r\n\r\nMeasurements\r\n\r\n29.\t Length Mass and Volume\r\n30.\t Area and Perimeter \r\n31.\tEstimating Volume\r\n32.\t Time\r\n33.\t Money\r\n34.\t Solve Problems\r\n\r\nGeometry\r\n\r\n35.\t Angles\r\n36.\tNets\r\n37.\t Coordinates\r\n38.\t Reflection\r\n\r\nStatistics\r\n\r\n39.\tCharts\r\n\r\nTEST RESULTS\r\nOn the completion of each test the user is given a summary of questions answered correctly and incorrectly, the percentage achieved in the test and the time taken on each test.
